23a3('bum): yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i gso sbyin la yang dag par sprul ba yin/ yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i gso sbyin gyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang yan lag brgyad pa
23a4('bum): ldan pa'i gso sbyin la nye bar gnas pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang bslab pa'i gnas lnga yang dag par 'dzin pa yin/ gzhan yang bslab
23a5('bum): pa'i gnas lnga la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bslab pa'i gnas lnga'i legs brjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang bslab pa'i gnas lnga la yang dag par 'dzin pa de dag gi legs pa
23a6('bum): rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ sems can gzhan yang bsam gtan dang po la yang dag par skul ba yin pa bsam/
23a7('bum): gtan dang po'i legs brjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs brjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang
23b1('bum): bsam gtan gnyis pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ ga'an yang bsam gtan gnyis pa la yang dag par bsgral pa yin/ bsam gtan gnyis pa'i legs rjong ba yin/ seMs /
23b2('bum): gzhan gang bsam gtan gnyis pa la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs brtad cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin+da/ bdag kyang bsam gtan gsum pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yin
23b3('bum): gzhan yang bsam gtan gsum pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bsam gtan gsum pa'i legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang bsam gtan gsum pa lnga snyoms pa
23b4('bum): 'jug pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang bsam gtan bzhi pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang bsam gtan gzhi pa la yang dag
23b5('bum): par skul ba yin/ bsam gtan bzhi pa'i legs parjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang bsam gtan bzhi pa la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs brjod cing mthun pas
23b6('bum): dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang byams pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang byams pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ byams pa'i legs parjod pa yin/ sems can
23b7('bum): gzhan gang byams pa la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang snying rje la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang snying rje la yang
24a1('bum): dag par skul ba yin/ snying rje'i legs brjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang snying rje la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod/
24a2('bum): pa yin/ bdag kyang dga' ba la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang dga' ba la yang dag par skul ba yin/ dga' ba'i legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang dga' ba
24a3('bum): la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang btang snyoms la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang btang snyoms la yang dag par
24a4('bum): skul ba yin/ btang snyoms kyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang btang snyom la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs parjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang nam/
24a5('bum): mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la yang dag par skul ba yin/ nam mkha' mtha' yos skye mched kyi legs brjod/
24a6('bum): pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang rnam shes mtha' yas skye
24a7('bum): mched la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched la yang dag par skul ba yin/ rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan
24b1('bum): gang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang cung zad med pa'i skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa yin//
24b2('bum): gzhan yang cung zad med pa'i skye mched la yang dag par skul pa yin/ cung zad med pa'i skye mched kyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang cung zad med pa'i skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa
24b3('bum): de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun par dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang 'du shes me de 'du shes med min skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mchedan/
24b4('bum): la yang dag par skul ba yin/ 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa de
24b5('bum): ngag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ dran
24b6('bum): panye bar gzhag pa rnams kyi legs pa rjod pa yin no// sems can gzhan gang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams sgoms pa de dag kyi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang yang dag
24b7('bum): par spong ba rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang yang dag par spong ba rnams la yang dag par stsal ba yin/ yang dag par spong ba rnams kyi legs brjod pa yin/ sems cad gzhan gang yang dag
25a1('bum): par spong ba rnams sgom pa de dag gi legs brjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang
25a2('bum): pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyi legs pa brjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sgom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga'
25a3('bum): bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang dbang po rnams skam pa yin/ gzhan yang dbang po rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ dbang po rnams kyi legs parjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang dbang po
25a4('bum): rnams sgom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang stobs rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stobs rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ stobs rnams kyi legs
25a5('bum): brjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang stobs rnams sgom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang byang chub
25a6('bum): kyi yan lag rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams sgom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing
25a7('bum): mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ 'phags pa'i
25b1('bum): lam yan lag brgyad pa'i legs brjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa sgom pa de dag gi legs parjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyong pa yin// bdag kyang /
25b2('bum): rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la yang dag par skul ba yin/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum gyi legs parjod pa yin// sems can gzhan gang rnam

25b4('bum): yin/ rnam par thar pa brgyad kyi legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang rnam par thar pa brgyad sdom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang mthar gyi gnas/
25b5('bum): pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu'i legs pa/
25b6('bum): rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu sgom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang mngon par shes pa lnga sgom pa
25b7('bum): yin/ gzhan yang mngon par shes pa lnga la yang dag par skul ba yin/ mngon par shes pa lnga'i legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang mngon par shes pa lnga sgom pa de dag gi legs pa
26a1('bum): rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang ting nge 'dzin rnams la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par

26a4('bum): gzungs kyi sgo rnams sgom pa de dag gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i

26b1('bum): so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la yang dag par skul ba yin/ so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi'i legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi sgom pa de dag gi leg/

26b7('bum): mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la yang dag par skul ba yin/ mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi legs par rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis sgrub pa de dag
27a1('bum): gi legs pa rjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ bdag kyang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu sgrub pa yin/ gzhan yang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu la yang dag par skul ba
27a2('bum): yin/ dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu'i legs pa rjod pa yin/ sems can gzhan gang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu sgrub pa de dag gi legs parjod cing mthun pas dga' bar spyod pa yin/ rab 'byor
27a3('bum): gal te chos kyi dbyings mngon ji ltar phyis kyang de bzhin ma yin nam/ bar du'ang de bzhin ma yin du zin na ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i

29b1('bum): med kyis/ rigs kyi bu soms dang / gang gi srog gcad par bya ba'i srog chags dang / gang gi skyog gcad par bya ba de lta bu'i chos kyang gang zhig yin/ gang ma byin par blang ba dang / ma byin

30a1('bum): par mthong ba de lta bu'i chos kyang gang zhig yin zhes ston cing / tshul khrims la 'god de/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thabs mkhas pa de lta bu dang
30a2('bum): ldan pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed do// des de la sbyin pa dang tshul khrims kyi 'bras bu bstan te/ sbyin pa'i 'bras bu dang / tshul khrims
30a3('bum): kyi 'bras bu de'ang ngo bo nyid kyis stong par bstan paso// rigs kyi bu des sbyin pa dang / tshul khrims kyi 'bras bu'i ngo bo nyid kyis stong par rig nas/ de la mngon par zhen por mi byed do// mngon par zhen pa med
30a4('bum): pas/ 'khrugs par mi 'gyur zhing shes rab skyed do// shes rab des kyang bag la nyal ba dang / kun nas ldang ba thams cad nas/ phung po ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yongs su mya ngan
30a5('bum): las 'das te/ de'ang 'jig rten gyi tha snyad kyi/ don dam par ni ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ stong pa nyid la gang yongs su mya ngan las 'dara' ba'am/ yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya ba de lta bur
30a6('bum): chos gang yang mi dmigs te/ de'i mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya ba ni/ 'di lta ste/ mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do// rab 'byor gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
30a7('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sems can phan tshun gnod par sems shing 'khrugs par gyur pa dang ldan pa dag mthong na/ 'di skad du 'dems shing ston te/ rigs kyi bu bzod pa sgrub
30b1('bum): shig/ bzod pa sgoms shig/ nges pa dang / sems zhi ba dang / dang du sems pa'i ngang tshul can du gyis shig/ gang gnod par byed pa dang / gang gis gnod par bya ba dang / gang la gnod par bya ba'i chos
30b2('bum): de dag ni thams cad kyang rang bzhin gyis stong pa yin gyis/ rigs kyi bu gnod par byed pa ni su yod/ gnod par ni su la bya/ cis ni gnod par bya soms dang / chos de dag thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong pa
30b3('bum): ste/ rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni/ nam yang mi stong pa mi 'gyur te// de ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ma mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ma byas so// rang sangs rgyas rnams
30b4('bum): kyis ma byas so// nyan thos rnams kyis ma byas so// lha rnams kyis ma byas so// klu rnams kyis ma byas so// gnod sbyin rnams kyis ma byas so// dri za rnams kyis ma byas so// lha ma yin rnams
30b5('bum): kyis ma byas so// nam mkha' lding rnams kyis ma byas so// mi 'am ci rnams kyis ma byas so// lto 'phye chen po rnams kyis ma byas so// rgyal chen bzhi'i rigs kyi lha rnams kyis ma byas so// sum
30b6('bum): cu rtsa gsum dang / mtshe ma dang / dga' ldan dang / 'phrul dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang / tshangs pa dang / dge rgyas dang / gnas gtsang ma dang / nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang / rnam
30b7('bum): shes mtha' yas skye mched dang / cung zad med pa'i skye mched dang / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi lha rnams kyis ma byas te/ de ni rtag par yang rang bzhin gyis stong pa'o// rang bzhin gyis
31a1('bum): stong pa ni su la'ang gnod par mi byed do zhes nas/ rab 'byor de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod cing / sems can rnams
31a2('bum): thabs mkhas pas rang bzhin stong pa nyid dang / rgyu dang 'bras bu la sbyor te/ rang bzhi ni stong pa nyid la bkod cing / rim gyis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par ston to//
31a3('bum): yang dag par skul lo// yang dag par bzengs bstod do// yang dag par dga' bar byed do// gzhog go// 'dul lo// rab tu 'god do// derang 'jig rten gyi tha snyad kyi/ don dam par ni
31a4('bum): ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gang thob par byed pa dang / gang gis thob par bya ba dang / gang thob par bya ba dang / gang thob par bya ba gang yang med do// rab 'byor 'di
31a5('bum): ni yang dag pa'i mtha' stong pa nyid de/ de la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems can rnams kyi don du gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod de/ de la sems can du
31a6('bum): dmigs pa med do// sems can du gdags par dmigs pa med do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar chos thams cad ni sems can gyis dben pa'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang
31a7('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs mkhas pas sems can le lo can brtson 'grus rung ba dag mthong na/ 'di ltar lus dang sems
31b1('bum): sde brtson 'grus pa yang dag par sprul te/ phyogs kyi bu dag rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid la ni chos gang yang zhum zhing le lor 'gyur ba 'am/ glang la zhum zhing kyi yor 'gyurab 'ang/ gang gis rdus ring
31b2('bum): le lor 'gyur ba 'am/ gang zhum zhong la lor 'gyur ba'i chos gang yang med de/ chos de dag ni thams cad kyang rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid las mi 'da' ba yin gyis/ lus dang sems kyi brtson 'grus
31b3('bum): skyed la/ le lor bor te/ dge ba'i chos sbyin pa 'am/ tshul khrims sam/ bzod pa 'am/ brtson 'grus sam/ bsam gtan nam/ shes rab bam/ nang stong pa nyid dam/ phye stong pa nyid dam/
31b4('bum): phyi nang stong pa nyid dam/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dam/ chen po stong pa nyid dam/ don dam pa stong pa nyid dam/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid dam/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid dam/ mtha' las 'das pa sngo
31b5('bum): bo nyid dam/ thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid dam/ dor ba med pa stong pa nyid dmya/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid dam/ chos thams cad stong pa nyid dam/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid dam/ mi dmigs pa
31b6('bum): stong pa nyid dam/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid dam/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dam/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dam/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams sam/ yang dag par spong ba rnams sam/

32a1('bum): bsam gtan rnams sam/ tshad med pa rnams sam/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams sam/ rnam par thar pa rnams sam/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par
32a2('bum): 'jug pa rnams sam/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa 'am/ mngon par shes pa rnams sam/ ting nge 'dzin rnams sam/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams sam
32a3('bum): de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams sam/ mi 'jigs pa rnams sam/ so so yang dag par rigs pa rnams sam/ byams pa chen po 'am/ snying rje chen po 'am/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa de dag la
32a4('bum): brtson par gyis shig/ rigs kyi bu dag stong pa nyid kyis chos de dag thams cad sgrib pa med par rtogs shig/ sgribs pa med pa'i chos la zhum par 'gyur ba gang yang med do zhes/ rab 'byor de ltar byang
32a5('bum): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs mkhas pas sems can rnams la rang bzhin stong pa nyid yang dag par ston to// yang dag par skul lo// /
32a6('bum): yang dag par gzengs bstod do// yang dag par dga' bar byed do// gzhog go/ 'dul lo// rab tu 'god do// ci nas kyang gnyis la mi gnas pa de ltar rab tu 'god do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rang
32a7('bum): bzhin stong pa nyid ni gnyis su med de gnyis su byar med do// gnyis su med pa'i chos ni gang la'ang gnas pa med do// rab 'byor gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha/
32b1('bum): rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs mkhas pas sems can rnams rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyi brtson 'grus la 'dems shing rjes su ston te/ tshur rigs kyi bu sbyin pa 'am/ tshul khrims sam/ bzod/
32b2('bum): ba 'am/ brtson 'grus sam/ bsam gtan nam/ shes rab bam/ nang stong pa nyid dam/ phyi stong pa nyid dam/ phyi nang stong pa nyid dam/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dam/ chen po stong pa nyid dam/
32b3('bum): don dam pa stong pa nyid dam/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid dam/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid dam/ mthar las 'das pa stong pa nyid dam/ thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid dam/ dor ba med pa stong pa nyid

33b2('bum): g.yeng ba 'am/ rtse gcig tu 'gyur ba'i chos gang yang dmigs su med do// khyod kyis ting nge 'dzin de la gnas te/ rang bzhir stong pa nyid la spyad na/ lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyis dge

33b4('bum): spyod dam/ phyi stong pa nyid la spyod dam/ phyi nang stong pa nyid la spyod dam/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la spyod dam/ chen po stong pa nyid la spyod dam/ don dam pa stong pa nyid la spyod dam/ 'dus byas stong pa

34b6('bum): rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par gzungs thob cing / lus kyi dbang po'am/ ngag gi dbang po 'am/ yid kyi dbang po ma nyam pa yin/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
34b7('bum): des rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shin tu bsgoms pas/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shin tu sgoms pa des/ lam thams cad shin tu bsgoms par 'gyur te/
35a1('bum): nyan thos kyi lam mam/ rang sangs rgyas kyi lam mam/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam mam/ sangs rgyas kyi lam shin tu bsgoms par 'gyur/ mngon par shes pa gang byang chub

35a6('bum): shing rjes su ston te/ tshur rigs kyi bu lus dang ngag gam/ yid kyis las gang ci byed kyang rung ste/ de thams cad rang bzhin stong pa nyid du rtogs shig dang / khyod kyi lam thams cad bdud rtsir

35b1('bum): phyir zhe na/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid las yongs su nyams pa'i chos kyang gang yang med do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di lta rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid

36b1('bum): gzhan yang nung zad med pa'i skye brjed kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'du shes me 'du shes med mi skye mched kyi stobs par ma gru pa la snyoms pa 'jug pa snyen/ gan
36b2('bum): yang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par sprul pa yin/ bdag kyang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang sbyin pa'i pha rol du phyin pa la yang
36b3('bum): dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin+da/ gzhan yang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdog kyang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin

36b7('bum): yin/ bdag kyang phyi stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang phyi stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang phyi nang stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang phyi nang stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba
37a1('bum): yin/ bdag kyang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang chen po stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/
37a2('bum): gzhan yang chen po stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang don dam pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang don dam pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'dus byas stong
37a3('bum): pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'dus byas stong pa nyid lnga yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba
37a4('bum): yin// bdag kyang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/
37a5('bum): gzhan yang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dor ba med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/
37a6('bum): bdag kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rang bzhin stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang chos thams cad stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang chos thams cad stong pa
37a7('bum): nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid/
37b1('bum): sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par stsal ba yin/ bdag kyang dngos po med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dngos po meng pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/
37b2('bum): bdag kyang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dngos po med pa'i
37b3('bum): ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dran pa nye bar gnag pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang yang dag/
37b4('bum): par spong ba rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang yang dag par spong ba rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la yang /
37b5('bum): dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dbang po rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dbang po rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang stobs rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stobs rnams la
37b6('bum): yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag
37b7('bum): brgyad pasgom pa yin pa gzhan yang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam par thar pa'i sgo
38a1('bum): gsum la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag
38a2('bum): kyang rnam par thar pa brgyad la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam par thar pa brgyad la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mthar
38a3('bum): gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mngon par shes pa rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mngon par shes pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag
38a4('bum): kyang ting nge 'dzin rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang ting nge 'dzin rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang gzungs kyi sgo rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang gzungs kyi sgo rnams la yang
38a5('bum): dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi 'jigs pa bzhi la
38a6('bum): slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mi 'jigs pa bzhi la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la yang dag par skul
38a7('bum): ba yin/ bdag kyang byams pa chen po la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang byams pa chen po la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang snying rje chen po la slob pa yin pa gzhan yang snying rje chen po la yang dag par
38b1('bum): skul ba yin/ bdag kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la slob pa yin/ gzhan yangasas rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la yang dag pa sprul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi chen po'i mtshan sum
38b2('bum): cu rtsa gnyis la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dpe byad bzang po brgyad nul sgrib pa yin/ gzhan yang dpe byad bzang po bskyed
38b3('bum): rdul yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang lan
38b4('bum): cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la 'ang mi gnas ba yin/ gzhan yang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de
38b5('bum): la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang dgra bcom pa
38b6('bum): nyid la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang rang byang chub kyi shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rang byang chub la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
38b7('bum): kyi lam skyed pa yin/ gzhan yang lam de la 'dems shing rjes su ston pa dang / gzhog cing 'dul ba dang 'god pa yin te/ rab 'byor de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha
39a1('bum): rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sems dang po bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung ste/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gnas shing sems can+da rnams kyi don byed pa'i tshe/ nam yang lus med
39a2('bum): par gnas pa ma yin no// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te de ltar chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis stong pa lags na/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la ni sems can yang mi dmigs
39a3('bum): chos kyang mi dmigs/ chos ma lags pa'ang mi dmigs na/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi don du yang dag par 'jug pa
39a4('bum): lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ ji skad du smras pa bzhin no// chos thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong pa ste/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la
39a5('bum): ni/ sems can mi dmigs so// chos mi dmigs so// chos ma yin pa mi dmigs so// rab 'byor gal te chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis stong pa zhig ma yin na ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems
39a6('bum): dpa' chen po 'ang rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gnas par mi 'gyur te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas kyang chos rnams rang bzhin gyi stong par mi ston to//
39a7('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong pa'i chos de dag kyang gang zhe na/ rab 'byor gzugs ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du shes ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du byed ni rang bzhin gyis/
39b1('bum): sbyong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus
39b2('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor gzugs ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sgra ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dri ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ro ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //
39b3('bum): reg ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig gi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i rnam par shes pa rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i rnam par shes
39b4('bum): pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis spong ngo // yid kyi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig
39b5('bum): gi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //
39b6('bum): lus kyi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus te
39b7('bum): reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i 'dus te reg pa ni rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi
40a1('bum): lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni drang ba zhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor sa'i khams ni rang bzhin/
40a2('bum): gyis stong ngo // chu'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // me'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rlung gi khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // nam mkha'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam
40a3('bum): bar shes pa'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor ma rig pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du byed ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ming drang gzug
40a4('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // skye mched drug ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sred pa ni rang bzhin gyis spong ngo // len pa ni rang
40a5('bum): bzhin gyis stong ngo // srid pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // skye ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rga shi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshul
40a6('bum): khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bsam gtan gyi pha ram
40a7('bum): tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor nang stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //
40b1('bum): phyinang stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis sbyong ngo // stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis spyod do// chen po stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // don drab pa stong pa nyid rnying bzhin gyis stong //
40b2('bum): 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mtha' las 'das pa stong pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong
40b3('bum): pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //

40b5('bum): bzhin gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yang dag par spong ba rnams ni rang bzhin
40b6('bum): gyis stong ngo // rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dbang po rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // stobs rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // byang chub kyi yan lag rnams ni rang bzhin
40b7('bum): gyis stong ngo // 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bsam gtan rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshang
41a1('bum): med pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis spong ngo // rnam par thar ba rnams ni bzhin gyis sbyong ngo // A
41a2('bum): gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni rang bzhin gyis skyong ngo // mngon par shes pa rnams ni
41a3('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ting nge 'dzin rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzungs kyi sgo rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams ni rang bzhin gyis sbyong ngo // mi 'jigs
41a4('bum): pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // so so yang dag par rig pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // byams pa chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // snying rje chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dga' ba chen
41a5('bum): bo ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // btang snyoms chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //

41b1('bum): spongango / de bas dbyang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i rgyu/ phung po lan bden gyis stong pa zhes bya ba cos sto // skye med du
41b2('bum): gnyis ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// khams bco brgyad ni rang bzhin gyis stong nge zhes bya bar chos ston to// rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston

42a1('bum): 'jug pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis skyong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rnam pa sa pa brgyad ni rang bzhi gyis sbyong nas bya ba chos ston to// mas gyis banas pa'i snyoms pa

105a1('bum): na/ de ci'i slad du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bdag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs pa ste/ mngon par rdzog
105a2('bum): bar 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes bgyi bar sems par gyur/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub ni gnyis su dbyer ma mchis pa ste/ gnyis su med pas ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
105a3('bum): tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nus so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ byang chub ni gnyis su dbyer med pa ste/
105a4('bum): gnyis su spyod pa la byang chub med do// rab 'byor byang chub ni gnyis su med de gnyis su dbyer med pas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub ni byang chub bo// byang
105a5('bum): chub sems dpa' 'o zhes bya bar gnyis su bya ba la mi spyod de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub de ni/ gzugs la mi spyod do// tshor ba la mi spyod do// 'du shes
105a6('bum): la mi spyod do// 'du byed la mi spyod do// rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do// mig la mi spyod do// rna ba la mi spyod do// sna la mi spyod do// lce la mi spyod do// lus la mi spyod/
105a7('bum): yid la mi spyod do// gzugs la mi spyod do// sgra la mi spyod do// dri la mi spyod do// ro la mi spyod do// reg la mi spyod do// chos la mi spyod do// mig gi rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do//
105b1('bum): rna ba'i rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do// sna'i rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do// lce'i rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do// lus kyi rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do// yid kyi u bar shes
105b2('bum): ba la mi spyod do// mig gi 'dus te reg pa la mi spyod do// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa la mi spyod do// sna'i 'dus te reg pa la mi spyod do// lce'i 'dus te reg pa la mi spyod do// lus
105b3('bum): kyi 'dus te reg pa la mi spyod do// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa la mi spyod do// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la mi spyod do// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la mi
105b4('bum): spyod do// snga'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la mi spyod do// lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la mi spyod do// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la mi spyod do//
105b5('bum): di sbyi rgyas la snod // mas mim byed/ mas lams // smrasas me da / rdzug ma
105b6('bum): nam mkha'i khams la mi spyod do// rnam par shes pa'i khams la mi spyod do// ma rig pa la mi spong ngo // 'du byed la mi spyod do// rnam par shes pa la mi spyod do// ming dang gzug
105b7('bum): la mi spyod do// skye mched drug la mi spyod do// reg pa la mi spyod do// tshor ba la mi spyod do// sred pa la mi spyod do// len pa la mi spyod do// srid pa la mi spyod do// skye ba la mi spyod do//
106a1('bum): rga shi la mi spyod do// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyid pa la mi spyod do// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin bu la mi spyong ngo //
106a2('bum): brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do// bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do// nang stong pa nyid la mi spyod
106a3('bum): phyi stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// phyi nang stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// chen po stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// don dam pa stong pa nyid lo mi spyod do//
106a4('bum): 'dus byas stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la mi spyod do//
106a5('bum): dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// chos thams cad stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// mi dmigs pa stong
106a6('bum): pa nyid la mi spyod do// dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la mi spyod do// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa
106a7('bum): rnams la mi spyod do// yang dag par spong ba rnams la mi spyod do// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la mi spyod do// dbang po rnams la mi spyod do// stobs rnams la mi spyod do// byang chub kyi
106b1('bum): yan lag rnams la mi spyod do// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la mi spyod do// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la mi spyod do// bsam gtam rnams la mi spyod do// tshad med pa
106b2('bum): rnams la mi spyod do// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la mi spyod do// rnam par thar pa brgyad la mi spyod do// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms por 'jug pa dgu la
106b3('bum): mi spyong ngo // rnam par thar pa'i sgro stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la mi spyod do// mngon par shes pa rnams la mi spyod ngo // ting nge 'dzin rnams la mi spyod
106b4('bum): ngo// gzus kyi sgo rnams la mi spyod do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs brtu la mi spyod do// mi 'jigs pa bzhi la mi spyod do// so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la mi spyod do/
106b5('bum): rlabs pa chen po la mi spyod do// snying rje chen po la mi spyod do// sangs rgyas kyi chos mo 'dres pa bco brgyad la mi spyod do// rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la mi spyod do// lan ci
106b6('bum): phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu lo ma spyod do// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la mi spyod do// dgra bcom pa nyid la mi spyod do// rlung byang chub la mi spyod do// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid la
106b7('bum): mi spyod do// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la me spyad do/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub ni bdag gam bdag gir bya ba med pa ste/ bdag gis gzugs
107a1('bum): la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi gzugs so zhe 'am/ bdag gis tshor ba la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi tshor ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis 'du shes la spyad
107a2('bum): par bya'o zhe 'am bdag gi 'du shes so zhe 'am/ bdag gis 'du byed la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi 'du byed do zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam par shes pa la spyang par bya'o zhe 'pha
107a3('bum): bdag gis rnam par shes pa'o zhe 'amabadag gis mig la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi mig go zhe 'am/ bdag gis rna ba la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rna ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag
107a4('bum): gis sna la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi snga'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis lce la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi lce'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis lus la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi lus so zhe
107a5('bum): 'am/ bdag gis yid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi yid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis gzugs la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi gzugs so zhe 'am/ bdag gis sgra la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/
107a6('bum): bdag gi sba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis dril spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi dri'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis ro la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi ro'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi reg la spyad par bya'o zhe
107a7('bum): 'am/ bdag gi reg go zhe 'am/ bdag gis chos la spyang bar bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi chos so zhe 'am/ bdag gis mig gi rnam par shes pa la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi mig gi rnam
107b1('bum): par shes pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gi mig gi rnam par shes pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gis rna ba'i rnam par shes pa la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'o/ nu'am/ bdag gis

107b3('bum): zhe 'am/ bdag gis lus kyi rnam par shes pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi lus kyi rnam par shes pa'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis yid kyi rnam par shes pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag

107b6('bum): to reg pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi lce'i 'dus te reg pa'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis lus kyi 'dus te rig pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'o zhe 'am
107b7('bum): bdag gis yid kyi 'dus te reg pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis
108a1('bum): mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rna ba'i 'dus te rdeg pa'i
108a2('bum): rkyen gyis tshor ba'o zhe'am/ bdag gis sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la spyang bar bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi sde'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis tshor ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis kye'i 'dus te/
108a3('bum): reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi lha'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkye mgyis tshor ba'o zhe'am/ bdag gis lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la spyad par bya'o na'am/
108a4('bum): bdag gi lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis cho
108a5('bum): ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis sa'i khams la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi sa'i khams so zhe 'am/ bdag gis chu'i khams la spyod par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi chu'i khams so zhe'am
108a6('bum): bdag gis me'i khams la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi me'i khams so zhe 'am/ bdag gis rlung gi khams la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rlung gi khams so zhe 'am/ bdag gis
108a7('bum): nam mkha'i khams la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi nam mkha'i khams so zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam par shes pa'i khams la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rnam par shes pa'i khams so zhe'am/
108b1('bum): bdag gis ma rig pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi ma rig pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gis 'du byed la spyad par byara'o na 'am/ bdag gi 'du byed do zhe'am/ bdag gis rnam par shes pa la
108b2('bum): spyang bar bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rnam par shes pa'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis ming dang gzugs la spyad par byal ni 'am/ bdag gi ming dang gzugs so zhe 'am/ bdag gis skye mched drug la spyang

109a1('bum): brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gis bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyad

109a3('bum): 'am/ bdag gis nang stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi nang stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis phyi stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi phyi stong pa nyid do zhe'am/

109a5('bum): nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis chen po stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi chen po stong pa nyid do zhe 'am bdag gis don dam pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag
109a6('bum): gi don dam pa stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis 'dus byas stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi 'dus byas stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la
109a7('bum): spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do zhe'am/
109b1('bum): bdag gis thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do zhe'am/ bdag gis dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am
109b2('bum): bdag gi dor ba med pa stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis rang bzhin stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rang bzhin stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis chos thams cad stong pa nyid la
109b3('bum): spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi chos thams cad stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid do zhe
109b4('bum): 'am/ bdag gis mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag
109b5('bum): gi dngos po med pa stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa
109b6('bum): nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi dran pa nye bar
109b7('bum): gzhag pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis yang dag par spong ba bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi yang dag par spong ba bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o/
110a1('bum): zhe 'amabadag gi rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis dbang po lnga la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi dbang po lnga'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis stobs lnga la
110a2('bum): spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi stobs lnga'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis byang chub kyi yan lag bdun la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi byang chub kyi yan lag bdun no zhe 'am/ bdag gis
110a3('bum): 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/
110a4('bum): bdag gi 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis bsam gtan bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi bsam gtan bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis tshad med pa bzhi la
110a5('bum): spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi tshad med pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ gdag gi gzugs med pa'i snyoms
110a6('bum): par 'jug pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam par thar pa brgyad la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rnam par thar pa brgyad do zhe 'am/ bdag gis mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug
110a7('bum): ba dgu la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang /
110b1('bum): smon pa med pa la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gis mngon par shes pa rnams la spyad/
110b2('bum): par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi mngon par shes pa rnams so zhe 'am/ bdag gis ting nge 'dzin rnams la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi ting nge 'dzin rnams so zhe'am/ bdag gis
110b3('bum): gzungs kyi sgo rnams la spyad par bya'o na 'am/ bdag gi gzungs kyi sgo rnams so zhe'am/ bdag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi de
110b4('bum): bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis mi 'jigs pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi mi 'jigs pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis so so yang dag par
110b5('bum): rig pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis byams pa chen po la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi byams pa chen po'o zhe 'am/
110b6('bum): bdag gis snying rje chen po la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi snying rje chen po'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi
110b7('bum): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad do zhe 'am/ bdag gis rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'o zhe 'am
111a1('bum): bdag gis lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu
111a2('bum): la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis dgra bcom pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi dgra bcom pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis
111a3('bum): rang byang chub la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rang byang chub bo zhe 'am/ bdag gis lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid do/
111a4('bum): zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do zhe'am/ bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
111a5('bum): byang chub la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub bo zhes bya bar bdag dang bdag gir byed pa med do// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
111a6('bum): chen po'i byang chub ni 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod/ mi 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod do// rab 'byor gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang
111a7('bum): chub 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod/ mi 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub ci la spyod pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
111b1('bum): pa/ rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems de bzhin gshegs pas sprul pa'i byang chub 'dzin pa 'am/ mi 'dzin pa 'am/ ci la'ang spyod pa yod dam/ gsol ba/ bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags
111b2('bum): so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ dgra bcom pa'i rmi lam gyi blo 'dzin pa 'om/ mi 'dzin pa gang la'ang spyod dam/ gsol pa
111b3('bum): bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags te/ bcom ldan 'das dgra bcom pa la long yang nyal ba ma mchis na/ de'i rmi lam gyi blo 'dzin pa 'am/ mi 'dzin pa la spyod par 'gyur ba lhag la
111b4('bum): mchis/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub kyang 'dzin pa 'am/ mi 'dzin pa la spyod pa med do//
111b5('bum): gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod/ mi 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod/ gzugs la'ang mi
111b6('bum): spyod/ tshor ba la'ang mi spyod/ 'du shes la'ang mi spyod/ 'du byed la'ang mi spyod do// rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ mig la'ang mi spyod/ rna ba la'ang mi spyod/ sna la'ang mi spyod//
111b7('bum): lho la'ang mi spyod/ lus la'ang mi spyod/ yid la'ang mi spyod/ gzugs la 'ong mi spyod/ sgra la'ang mi spyod/ dri la'ang mi spyod/ ro la 'ang mi spyod/ reg la'ang mi spyod/ chos la 'a
112a1('bum): mi spyod/ mig gi rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ rna ba'i rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ sku'i rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ lce'i rnam par shes pa la'ang mi
112a2('bum): spyod/ lus kyi rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa
112a3('bum): la'ang mi spyod/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la'ang mi
112a4('bum): spyod/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la'ang mi spyod sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la'ang mi spyod/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la'ang mi spyod/

112a6('bum): khams la'ang mi spyod/ rlung gi khams la'ang mi spyod/ nam mkha'i khams la'ang mi spyod/ rnam par shes pa'i khams la'ang mi spyod/ ma rig pa la'ang mi spyod/ 'du byed la'ang mi spyod//

112b1('bum): pa la'ang mi spyod/ srid pa la'ang mi spyodaskye ba la'ang mi spyod/ rga shI la'ang mi spyod/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang mi spyod/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang mi spyod
112b2('bum): bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang mi spyod/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la 'jo mi spyod/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin po la'ang mi spyod shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang

113a7('bum): byang chub la'ang mi spyod/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la'ang mi spyod na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po pha rol tu phyin pa

132a4('bum): mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa sgom pa'ang mi dmigs chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur/
132a5('bum): te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na/ thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs
132a6('bum): par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ mngon par shes pa rnams slob yang / mngon par
132a7('bum): shes pa rnams dang / mngon par shes pa sgom pa'ang mi dmigs chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob
132b1('bum): bar 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar myong na/ thabs mkhas pas bla ma med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
132b2('bum): par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nam byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ ting nge 'dzin rnams sgom yang
132b3('bum): ting nge 'dzin rnams dang / ting nge 'dzin sgom pa'ang mi dmigs chos dri gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi la ma thob
132b4('bum): bar 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na/ thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
132b5('bum): tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nam byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ gzungs kyi sgo rnam
132b6('bum): sgom yang gzungs kyi sgo rnams dang / gzungs kyi sgo sgom pa'ang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang
132b7('bum): chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
133a1('bum): pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs pa'i 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nam byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i//
133a2('bum): de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu sgom yang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs sgom pa'ang mi dmigs chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang
133a3('bum): mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la
133a4('bum): de ltar spyod na thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nas byang chub sems dpa' sems
133a5('bum): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ mi 'jigs pa bani sgom yang mi 'jigs pa rnams dang / mi 'jigs pa sgom pa'ang mi dmigs chos de gnyis
133a6('bum): las gzhan du rang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha
133a7('bum): rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod da/ thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs pa 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nas byang chub
133b1('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod ba'i tshe/ so so yang dag par rig pa bani sgom yang / sa mo yang dag par rig pa rnams dang / so so yang dag
133b2('bum): bar rig pa sgom pa'ang mi dmigs chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor
133b3('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na/ thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs por
133b4('bum): 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe snying rje chen po sgom yang / snying rje chen po dang /

133b6('bum): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na/ thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o//
133b7('bum): rab 'byor gzhan yang nam byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad sgom yang / sangs rgyas kyi chos
134a1('bum): ma 'dres pa rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa sgom pa'ang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod ma/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sem/
134a2('bum): dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na thabs mkhas pas bla na med pa yang /
134a3('bum): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das/
134a4('bum): ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ byang chub kyi lam la brtson par bgyis pa lags bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/
134a5('bum): shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs mkhas pas gzugs mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir ni/
134a6('bum): de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i gzugs la ngo bo nyid med do// tshor ba mi sbyor mi byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i tshor ba la
134a7('bum): ngo bo nyid med do// 'du shes mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i 'du shes la ngo bo nyid med do// 'du byed mi sbyor mi 'byed de

138b3('bum): do// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// dngos po med pa

140b1('bum): bgyi ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ji ltar mngon par 'grub par 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ma bslabs par ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bla na med
140b2('bum): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nus so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu de de bzhin te/ de de bzhin no//

140b4('bum): par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nus te/ de'ang thabs mkhas pas yin gyis/ thabs mi mkhas pas ma yin no// shA ra dwa ti'i bu gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
140b5('bum): chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ chos gang la la zhig gi ngo bo nyid dmigs na ni de'i phyir 'dzin par yang 'gyur na/ 'on te mi dmigs ni 'di ni gzugs so// 'di
140b6('bum): ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni 'du shes so// 'di ni 'du byed do// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya bar yang ci zhig gzung / 'di dag ni skye mched rnams so// 'di dag ni khams rnams so//

141a1('bum): ni reg pa'o// 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni sred pa'o// 'di ni len pa'o// 'di ni srid pa'o// 'di ni skye ba'o// 'di ni rga shi'o// 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa/

231a3('bum): pa nyid la gnas dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la gnas dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la gnas yang dag par spong ba rnams lags rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la gnas
231a4('bum): dbang po lnga la gnas stobs lnga la gnas/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la gnas 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la gnas 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la gnas/
231a5('bum): bsam gtan rnams la gnas/ tshad med pa rnams la gnas gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la gnas/ rnam par thar pa brgyad la gnas mthar gyis gnas/
231a6('bum): pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la gnas rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la gnas/ mngon par shes pa rnams la gnas
231a7('bum): ting nge 'dzin rnams la gnas gzungs kyi sgo rnams la gnas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la gnas mi 'jigs pa bzhi la gnas so so yang dag par rig pa
231b1('bum): ba'i la gnas byams pa chen po la gnas/ snying rje chen po la gnas sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco bkyang la gnas shing / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rjes su myog
231b2('bum): par byed de/ rab 'byor de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas shing / sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed de/ de ltar yong
231b3('bum): su smin par byas pa rnams ngan song gsum las yongs su thar pa nas/ 'khor ba thams cad kyi bar las yongs su thar ro// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa las le'u
231b4('bum): drug cu bdun no// de nas tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor 'di snyam du gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos de lta bu'i go bgo bar bya na/ de la
231b5('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub kyi lam ji lta bu zhig yod snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyi sems kyis yongs su rtog pazugs
231b6('bum): kyis thugs su chud nas tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rab 'byor sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo//
231b7('bum): rab 'byor tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems
232a1('bum): dpa' chen po'i las so// rab 'byor brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor bsam gtan
232a2('bum): gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo//
232a3('bum): rab 'byor nang stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor phyi stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor/
232a4('bum): phyi nang stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo//
232a5('bum): rab 'byor chen po stong pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor don dam pa stong pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo//
232a6('bum): rab 'byor 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
232a7('bum): po'i lam mo// rab 'byor mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid ni/
232b1('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni
232b2('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor rang gi mtshan nyid
232b3('bum): stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor
232b4('bum): ngom po med pa stong ba nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo//
232b5('bum): rab 'byor dngas pa med pa'i ngom nyid stong pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chem po'i lam ma// rab 'byor dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi ni byang chub sems dpa'
232b6('bum): sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor yang dag par spong ba bzhini/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhin/ bya chu
232b7('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor dbang po lnga ni / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pa'i lam mo// rab 'byor spobs lnga ni/ byang chub sems
233a1('bum): dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor byang chub kyi yan lag bdun ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor 'phags
233a2('bum): pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i

233a5('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab

233a7('bum): rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor ting nge 'dzin rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor gzung
233b1('bum): kyi sgo rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcuni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo/
233b2('bum): rab 'byor mi 'jigs pa bzhini byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i
233b3('bum): lam mo// rab 'byor byams pa chen po ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor snying rje chen po ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i
233b4('bum): lam mo// rab 'byor sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor gzhan yang chos thams cad ni/ byang chub
233b5('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i lam mo// rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ chos gang la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bslab par mi bya ba dang / gang la ma bslabs kyang
233b6('bum): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba de lta bu'i chos gang yang yod dam/ rab 'byor gang la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bslab par
233b7('bum): mi bya ba de lta bu'i chos gang yang med de/ chos thams cad la ma bslabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob par mi nus so//
234a1('bum): rab 'byor gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te chos thams cad stong pa nyid lags na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos thams cad la ji lta/
234a2('bum): bslab par bgyi ste/ bcom ldan 'das 'di snyed do zhes bgyi ba 'am/ 'di dag go zhes bgyi ba dang / 'jig rten pa'i chos ni 'di dag go// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos ni 'di dag go/
234a3('bum): zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos ni 'di dag go/ zag pa med pa'i chos ni 'di dag go// 'dus byas kyi chos ni 'di dag go// 'dus ma byas kyi chos ni 'di dag go// so so'i skye bo'i chos ni 'di dag go/

234a5('bum): gi byang chub sems dpa'i chos ni 'di dag go// sangs rgyas kyi chos ni 'di dag go zhes bgyi ba ni/ spros pa ma mchis pa 'phro bar bgyid pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/

234b1('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos thams cad la bslabs shing / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor khyod kyis gzhan

357b7('bum): 'di lta ste/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi dang / yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang / dbang po lnga dang / stobs lnga dang / byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dang / 'phags pa'i
358a1('bum): lam yan lag brgyad pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum dang / 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dang / stong pa nyid thams cad dang / rnam par thar pa brgyad dang / mthar gyis
358a2('bum): gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu dang / ting nge 'dzin thams cad dang / gzungs kyi sgo thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / so so yang dag par rig
358a3('bum): ba bzhi dang / byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang / de dag gi 'bras bu gang gis gang zag rgyun du zhugs pa dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba dang /

358a5('bum): sprul pa lags samabacom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor chos thams cad ni sprul pa ste/ de la la la ni nyan thos kyis sprul pa'o// la la ni rang sangs rgyas kyis sprul pa'o//
358a6('bum): la la ni byang chub sems dpas sprul pa'o// la la ni de bzhin gshegs pas sprul pa'o// la la ni nyon mongs pas sprul pa'o// la la ni las kyis sprul pa'o// rab 'byor rnam grangs des na/ chos thams
358a7('bum): cad ni sprul pa'o// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang spangs pa zhes bgyi ba rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu 'am/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu 'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu 'am/ dgra bcom pa
358b1('bum): nyid dam/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sa 'am/ sangs rgyas kyi sa 'am/ bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba thams cad spangs pa'i chos de dag kyang sprul pa lags sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
358b2('bum): ba/ rab 'byor bskyed pa 'am/ bkag pa'i chos gang ci'ang rung ste/ de thams cad ni sprul pa'o// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang ma sprul pa'i chos de dag gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das
358b3('bum): kyis bka' stsal pa/ chos gang la skye ba'ang med/ 'gag pa'ang med pa de ni ma sprul pa'o// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ mi mnyam
358b4('bum): pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa ste/ chos de ni ma sprul pa'o// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad du stong pa nyid las kyang mi g.yo la/ gnyis su'ang mi dmigs te/ chos gang yang
358b5('bum): stong pa nyid ma yin pa de lta bu med do zhes bka' stsal ba ltar na/ bcom ldan 'das mi mnyam pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'ang sprul par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa
358b6('bum): rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ rab 'byor chos thams cad ni stong pa ste/ de dag ni nyan thos kyis ma byas rang sangs rgyas kyis ma byas// byang chub sems dpa' sems
358b7('bum): dpa' chen pos ma byas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis ma byas te/ ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni mya ngan las 'das pa'o//
359a1('bum): rab 'byor gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das las dang po pa'i gang zag gis ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa nyid yongs su 'tshal bar bgyi na/ ji ltar gdams shing
359a2('bum): rjes su bstan par bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa rab 'byor ci sngon dngos po yod par gyur la/ phyis dngos po med par 'gyur ba yod dam/ rab 'byor/
359a3('bum): 'di la dngos po yod pa'ang med/ dngos po med pa'ang med/ ngo bo nyid kyang med/ gzhan gyi dngos po'ang med na/ de la gang yongs su shes par bya ba'i ngo bo nyid stong pa
359a4('bum): nyid ces bya ba lta yod par 'gyur re skan/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa las/ chos nyid mi 'gyur bar bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun cu gnyis so// /
359a5('bum): 'di ni bsam las dang / lha sa'i rig zing mtshams mi 'dar la sogs pa la gtugs nas zhus dag lan bcu drug byas pa'i rgyan gong gi 'bum nag mtshams mi 'dar/
359a6('bum): la phyi mo byas nas/ dag par gtugs pa'i 'bum sdig ma 'dres zhes bya ba'i gser 'bum bcu gnyis dum/ lo tsa ba chen po thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin grub kyi thugs dam la phyi mo bgyis nas//
